settlement, lending \u0026amp;amp; borrowing activity- and liaise directly with Treasury Management.\u0026lt;/span\u0026gt;\u0026lt;/li\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;li class=\u0026quot;li4\u0026quot;\u0026gt;\u0026lt;span class=\u0026quot;s1\u0026quot;\u0026gt;Provide inputs to compliance and risk teams to design pragmatic controls in this environment of changing regulatory landscape.\u0026lt;/span\u0026gt;\u0026lt;/li\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;li class=\u0026quot;li4\u0026quot;\u0026gt;\u0026lt;span class=\u0026quot;s1\u0026quot;\u0026gt;Adhere to established trade operations processes designed for regulatory compliance.\u0026lt;/span\u0026gt;\u0026lt;/li\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;li class=\u0026quot;li5\u0026quot;\u0026gt;\u0026lt;span class=\u0026quot;s1\u0026quot;\u0026gt;Liaise with Accounting and ensure proper trade and settlement data is provided to them on a timely basis.\u0026lt;/span\u0026gt;\u0026lt;/li\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;/ul\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;p class=\u0026quot;p3\u0026quot;\u0026gt;\u0026lt;strong\u0026gt;Requirements\u0026lt;/strong\u0026gt;\u0026lt;/p\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;ul class=\u0026quot;ul1\u0026quot;\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;li class=\u0026quot;li4\u0026quot;\u0026gt;\u0026lt;span class=\u0026quot;s1\u0026quot;\u0026gt;1-5 years of experience in a trading firm, hedge fund or bank\u0026lt;/span\u0026gt;\u0026lt;/li\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;li class=\u0026quot;li4\u0026quot;\u0026gt;\u0026lt;span class=\u0026quot;s1\u0026quot;\u0026gt;Superb self-management skills - you love organizing your work with the help of checklists and measuring your progress.\u0026lt;/span\u0026gt;\u0026lt;/li\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;li class=\u0026quot;li4\u0026quot;\u0026gt;\u0026lt;span class=\u0026quot;s1\u0026quot;\u0026gt;Previous experience working in fast-paced, high pressure environment\u0026lt;/span\u0026gt;\u0026lt;/li\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;li class=\u0026quot;li4\u0026quot;\u0026gt;\u0026lt;span class=\u0026quot;s1\u0026quot;\u0026gt;BA/BS in Finance, Accounting or a related field\u0026lt;/span\u0026gt;\u0026lt;/li\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;li class=\u0026quot;li5\u0026quot;\u0026gt;\u0026lt;span class=\u0026quot;s1\u0026quot;\u0026gt;Desire to become an expert on digital assets such as Bitcoin and Ethereum\u0026lt;/span\u0026gt;\u0026lt;/li\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;/ul\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;p class=\u0026quot;p1\u0026quot;\u0026gt;You will be required to gain an understanding of the broader responsibilities of cryptocurrency trade operations and the life cycle of institutional trading. You should strive to be the first point of contact for trade settlements and operations. You will have exposure to a wide range of functions in a complex and dynamic market. The ability to multitask and prioritize will be key, combined with management of critical day-to-day functions.\u0026lt;/p\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;p class=\u0026quot;p1\u0026quot;\u0026gt;\u0026lt;strong\u0026gt;Compensation\u0026lt;/strong\u0026gt;\u0026lt;/p\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;p class=\u0026quot;p1\u0026quot;\u0026gt;Base pay for this role is expected to be between $90,000 and $120,000 USD.
